create them in advance. For more information, please go to section about Field. Individual client is a natural person, as opposed to legal entity or a sole trader.\\n\\n### Endpoint\\n\\n```\\nPOST /admin/clients.json\\n```\\n\\n### Parameters\\n\\n| Name | Description |\\n| --- | --- |\\n| client\\\\[name\\\\]<br> required | name |\\n| client\\\\[surname\\\\]<br> required | surname |\\n| client\\\\[middlename\\\\]<br> required | middlename |\\n| client\\\\[registered\\\\] | if true, email and password are required |\\n| client\\\\[email\\\\] | email |\\n| client\\\\[password\\\\] | password at least 6 characters |\\n| client\\\\[phone\\\\] | phone number |\\n| client\\\\[subscribe\\\\] | set true to subscribe client for emails |\\n| client\\\\[client\\\\_group\\\\_id\\\\] | client group id |\\n| client\\\\[type\\\\] | Client::Individual, by default |\\n| client\\\\[ip\\\\_addr\\\\] | IP address |\\n| client\\\\[correspondent\\\\_account\\\\] | Correspondent account |\\n| client\\\\[settlement\\\\_account\\\\] | Settlement account |\\n| client\\\\[fields\\\\_values\\\\_attributes\\\\] | fields values array |\\n| client\\\\[fields\\\\_values\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[value\\\\] | value of field |\\n| client\\\\[fields\\\\_values\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[field\\\\_id\\\\] | field id |\\n| client\\\\[skip\\\\_send\\\\_mail\\\\] | set it true to skip sending email confirmation |\\n\\n### Request\\n\\n#### Route\\n\\n```\\nPOST /admin/clients.json\\n```\\n\\n#### Headers\\n\\n```http hljs\\nContent-Type: application/json\\nAuthorization: Basic ZGlnaXRhbC1nb29kczpjNTFjOTA3MDdhMTNjZTNmZmYyMTNhZmJiNWNkMTI3MA==\\n```\\n\\n#### Body\\n\\n```application/json hljs\\n{\\n  "client": {\\n    "name": "Ivan",\\n    "surname": "Ivanov",\\n "fields_values_attributes": [\\\\\\n      {\\\\\\n        "field_id": 186,\\\\\\n        "value": "text"\\\\\\n      }\\\\\\n    ]\\n  }\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### Response\\n\\n[Simulated DeliveryVariant\\n\\n## Create delivery\\\\_variant External\\n\\nDeliveryVariant::External is an external delivery variant.\\n\\n### Endpoint\\n\\n```\\nPOST /admin/delivery_variants.json\\n```\\n\\n### Parameters\\n\\n| Name | Description |\\n| --- | --- |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[title\\\\]<br> required | title |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[type\\\\]<br> required | DeliveryVariant::External, DeliveryVariant::Fixed, DeliveryVariant::LocationDepend, DeliveryVariant::MapZoneDelivery, DeliveryVariant::None, DeliveryVariant::OfficialEmsShipping, DeliveryVariant::OfficialFirstClass, DeliveryVariant::OfficialRussianpost, DeliveryVariant::PickUp, DeliveryVariant::PriceDepend |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[description\\\\] | description |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[position\\\\] | position |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[add\\\\_payment\\\\_gateways\\\\] | set true to add all payment variants |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\] | array of delivery locations |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[country\\\\] | Optional. Default: RU. It should be enabled in checkout options to be binded to shipping method. |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[region\\\\] | Required. Field Region should be enabled in checkout options to be binded to shipping method. Examples: "Ивановская", "Омская" |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[area\\\\] | Optional. Ignored if city present. Field Region should be filled. Examples: "Знаменский" |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[city\\\\] | Optional. Field Region should be filled. Examples: "Омск" |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[inverted\\\\] | false by default, if true this delivery variant will be available for all regions except passed in parameters \\\'country\\\', \\\'region\\\' and \\\'city\\\' |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[charge\\\\_up\\\\_to\\\\] | free on orders from given sum |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[javascript\\\\] | if needed, paste javascript to Endpoint\\n\\n```\\nPOST /admin/delivery_variants.json\\n```\\n\\n### Parameters\\n\\n| Name | Description |\\n| --- | --- |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[title\\\\]<br> required | title |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[type\\\\]<br> required | DeliveryVariant::External, DeliveryVariant::Fixed, DeliveryVariant::LocationDepend, DeliveryVariant::MapZoneDelivery, DeliveryVariant::None, DeliveryVariant::OfficialEmsShipping, DeliveryVariant::OfficialFirstClass, DeliveryVariant::OfficialRussianpost, DeliveryVariant::PickUp, DeliveryVariant::PriceDepend |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[description\\\\] | description |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[position\\\\] | position |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[add\\\\_payment\\\\_gateways\\\\] | set true to add all payment variants |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\] | array of delivery locations |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[country\\\\] | if shop has many countries, fill this field;it should be enabled in checkout options to be binded to shipping method |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[region\\\\] | field Region should be enabled in checkout options to be binded to shipping method |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[delivery\\\\_locations\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[city\\\\] | field Region should be filled |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[inverted\\\\] | false by default, if true this delivery variant will be available for all regions except passed in parameters \\\'country\\\', \\\'region\\\' and \\\'city\\\' |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[charge\\\\_up\\\\_to\\\\] | free on orders from given sum |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[min\\\\_price\\\\] | minimal delivery price |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[rules\\\\_attributes\\\\] | array of rules define delivery price depending on order sum and weight |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[rules\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[price\\\\] | delivery price by a rule |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[rules\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[order\\\\_price\\\\] | order sum by a rule |\\n| delivery\\\\_variant\\\\[rules\\\\_attributes\\\\]\\\\[order\\\\_weight\\\\] | order weight by a rule |\\n\\n### Request\\n\\n#### Route\\n\\n```\\nPOST chains\\n\\n### Endpoint\\n\\n```\\nPOST /admin/redirects.json\\n```\\n\\n### Parameters\\n\\n| Name | Description |\\n| --- | --- |\\n| redirect\\\\[old\\\\_url\\\\]<br> required | old url |\\n| Response](/simulate/redirect/create_redirect_with_removing_redirect_chains_json)\\n\\n#### Status\\n\\n```http hljs\\n201\\n```\\n\\n#### Headers\\n\\n```http hljs\\nAPI-Usage-Limit:
